src="/wcsstore/TargetOpticalStorefrontAssetStore/images/pupillary-distance.jpg" aria-hidden="true" role="presentation" /><h3>what is it?</h3><p>Pupillary distance measures the space (in millimeters) between the pupils of your eyes.</p><h3>where can I find it?</h3><p>On previous eyewear receipts or your prescription. Or measure it yourself with our handy PD ruler.</p><a target="_blank" href="/wcsstore/TargetOpticalStorefrontAssetStore/Attachment/TO-PD Ruler-FINAL-062113.pdf">download PD ruler</a></div></div></div><div id="MultiplePDModal" accordion="block-rx"
